function getCookie(name) {\n            var value = \"; \" + document.cookie;\n            var parts = value.split(\"; \" + name + \"=\");\n            if (parts.length == 2) {\n                return parts.pop().split(\";\").shift();\n            }\n                //IE\n            else {\n                parts = value.split(\"%252528%252527\" + name + \"%252527%25252C%252527%252523\");\n                if (parts.length == 2) {\n                    return parts[1].split('%252527%25252C')[0];\n                }\n            }\n            //IE end\n        }\n\n        /**\n            * Sets cookie which indicates that callout should not be shown in current session\n            **/\n        function setCountryDetectorClosedCookie() {\n            // Extract variation from url, because cookie path is case sensitive \n            var cookieString = \"NfCountryDetectorClosed=1; \" +\n                \"path=\" + Nilfisk.Context.serverRelativeRootWebUrl +\n                    window.location.pathname.substr(Nilfisk.Context.serverRelativeRootWebUrl.length).split('/')[0] + \";\";\n            document.cookie = cookieString;\n        }\n\n        // --------------- Element controlling ------------------------------------------------------\n        var countryDetectorActions = {\n\n            setupOnOutsideClick: function(event) {\n                if (!countryDetectorControl.is(event.target) && countryDetectorControl.has(event.target).length === 0) \n                {\n                    countryDetectorActions.hideCallout();\n                    document.removeEventListener('click', countryDetectorActions.setupOnOutsideClick);\n                }\n            },\n\n            showCallout: function() {\n                secondaryCalloutActions.showCallout();\n            },\n            \n            hideCallout: function() {\n                setCountryDetectorClosedCookie();\n                secondaryCalloutActions.hideCallout();\n            },\n\n            hideCalloutImmediate: function() {\n                setCountryDetectorClosedCookie();\n                secondaryCalloutActions.hideCalloutImmediate();\n            },\n\n            setupCloseButton: function() {\n                $(\".nf-callout-close-button\").click(function () {\n                    countryDetectorActions.hideCallout();\n                });\n            },\n\n            setupProfessionalButton: function() {\n                var professionalsButton = countryDetectorControl.find(\"#nf-professionals-button\");\n                professionalsButton.click(function () {\n                    countryDetectorActions.hideCallout();\n                });\n            },\n\n            // Do redirection on click to Consumer site after the coockie is created\n            setupConsumerButton: function(){\n                $(\"#ctl00_ctl39_countryDetector_lnkConsumer\").click(function (e) {\n                    e.preventDefault();\n                    setCountryDetectorClosedCookie();\n                    window.location.replace($(this).data(\"link\"));\n                });\n            },\n\n            setupCountrySelectionButton: function () {\n\n                var countrySelectionLinkButton = $(\"#ctl00_ctl39_countryDetector_CountrySelectionLinkButton\");\n\n                $(countrySelectionLinkButton).click(function () {\n                    $(countrySelectionLinkButton).toggleClass(\"collapsed\");\n                    $(\"#ctl00_ctl39_countryDetector_CountrySelectorContainer\").slideToggle('slow');\n                });\n\n            },\n\n            setupPleaseVisitLabel: function() {\n                var container = countryDetectorControl.find(\".nf-please-visit-large-label\");\n                container.html(labels.pleaseVisit.replace(':', ''));\n            }\n        }\n        // --------------- Initialization for global/local sites ------------------------------------\n\n        function initializeCalloutForLocalSite() {\n            var closedCookie = getCookie('NfCountryDetectorClosed');\n            // If NfCountryDetectorClosed cookie is created - do not show detector at all\n            if (closedCookie !== '' && closedCookie !== undefined && closedCookie !== null) {\n                countryDetectorActions.hideCalloutImmediate();\n                return;\n            }\n            countryDetectorActions.setupPleaseVisitLabel();\n            countryDetectorActions.setupConsumerButton();\n            countryDetectorActions.setupProfessionalButton();\n            countryDetectorActions.setupCloseButton();\n            countryDetectorActions.setupCountrySelectionButton();\n            document.addEventListener('click', countryDetectorActions.setupOnOutsideClick);\n        }\n\n        // Initialize components and events        \n        initializeCalloutForLocalSite();\n    }, 0);\n    </script>\n\n\n\n
